                    INSERT /*+ BYPASS_RECURSIVE_CHECK */ INTO
                    "THH_C4C"."MV_PATID_CLINIC_COND_SRVCD" SELECT /*+ ORDERED */
                    greatest(t_userdiagbase.valid_from, nvl(tapbl.valid_from,
                    to_date(:"SYS_B_00", :"SYS_B_01"))) valid_from,            CASE
                         WHEN t_userdiagbase.valid_to IS NULL AND
                    tapbl.valid_to IS NULL THEN                TO_DATE(:"SYS_B_02",
                    :"SYS_B_03")              WHEN t_userdiagbase.valid_to IS NOT NULL AND
                                     tapbl.valid_to IS NOT NULL THEN
                    least(t_userdiagbase.valid_to, tapbl.valid_to)              WHEN
                    t_userdiagbase.valid_to IS NULL THEN                tapbl.valid_to
                            ELSE                t_userdiagbase.valid_to            END
                                       valid_to,            t_userdiagbase.mbur_id
                    member_id,            tapbl.srvc_id               srvcd,            --
                    CP-268     	   tapbl.APBL_RQTDDT_FROM      srv_date_from,     	
                    tapbl.APBL_RQTDDT_TO        srv_date_to          FROM
                    (SELECT                 nvl(tusr.usr_mrgemstr, tusr.usr_id) mbur_id,
                                 tmembdgis.umds_id,
                    greatest(tusr.valid_from, nvl(tmembdgis.valid_from,
                    to_date(:"SYS_B_04", :"SYS_B_05"))) valid_from,                 CASE
                                   WHEN tusr.valid_to IS NULL AND
                    tmembdgis.valid_to IS NULL THEN
                    TO_DATE(:"SYS_B_06", :"SYS_B_07")                   WHEN tusr.valid_to
                    IS NOT NULL AND                        tmembdgis.valid_to IS NOT NULL
                    THEN                     least(tusr.valid_to, tmembdgis.valid_to)
                                WHEN tusr.valid_to IS NULL THEN
                    tmembdgis.valid_to                   ELSE
                    tusr.valid_to                 END valid_to               FROM
                          a_usr tusr                 INNER JOIN
                    a_membdgisbase tmembdgis                   ON tusr.mbur_id =
                    tmembdgis.mdss_memb AND                      tusr.classtype=
                    :"SYS_B_08" AND                      (                       (
                                  tusr.valid_from >= tmembdgis.valid_from
                         AND                        (
                    tusr.valid_from <= tmembdgis.valid_to OR
                    tmembdgis.valid_to IS NULL                        )
                      )                       OR                       (
                        tusr.valid_from <= tmembdgis.valid_from                        AND
                                          (                         tusr.valid_to >=
                    tmembdgis.valid_from OR                         tusr.valid_to IS NULL
                                         )                       )                      )
                                       AND                      tusr.usr_obj_stt !=
                    :"SYS_B_09" AND                      tmembdgis.mbdb_obj_stt !=
                    :"SYS_B_10"                      AND NVL(tmembdgis.mdss_is_err,
                    :"SYS_B_11") = :"SYS_B_12"  -- is error filter            )
                    t_userdiagbase            INNER JOIN            (select a.*, b.srvc_id
                    from a_apbl a, a_apblsrvc b where a.apbl_id = b.apbl_id) tapbl
                        ON t_userdiagbase.umds_id = tapbl.msrv_srvcdgis AND
                    (                  (                   t_userdiagbase.valid_from >=
                    tapbl.valid_from                   AND                   (
                          t_userdiagbase.valid_from <= tapbl.valid_to OR
                    tapbl.valid_to IS NULL                   )                  )
                           OR                  (
                    t_userdiagbase.valid_from <= tapbl.valid_from                   AND
                                  (                    t_userdiagbase.valid_to >=
                    tapbl.valid_from OR                    t_userdiagbase.valid_to IS NULL
                                     )                  )                 )
                    AND                 tapbl.apbl_obj_stt != :"SYS_B_13"
                    AND NVL(tapbl.apbl_is_err, :"SYS_B_14") = :"SYS_B_15"  -- is error

                    t_mdclclm.mclm_frstdt_of_srvc          valid_from,
                    NVL(t_mdclclm.mclm_las_dt_of_srvc,
